\"text\": \"The Grafana unified alerting (ngalert) subsystem is implemented under pkg/services/ngalert/ in the sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec repository. The main entry point is ngalert.go which defines the AlertNG service that wires all subsystems together.\\n\\n**Core Components:**\\n\\n1. **Alert Rule Storage** (pkg/services/ngalert/store/): The store package implements alert rule persistence (alert_rule.go, instance_database.go, proto_instance_database.go), Alertmanager config storage (alertmanager.go), admin configuration (admin_configuration.go), image storage (image.go), namespace/org management (namespace.go, org.go), provisioning metadata (provisioning_store.go), and range-to-instant query support (range_to_instant.go). Uses a protobuf schema (store/proto/v1/alert_rule_state.pb.go) for alert instance serialization.\\n\\n2. **Scheduler** (pkg/services/ngalert/schedule/): The schedule package drives periodic alert rule evaluation. schedule.go contains the main scheduler loop, alert_rule.go defines the per-rule goroutine handling alert rules, recording_rule.go handles recording rules, registry.go manages active rule registrations, fetcher.go loads rules from store, jitter.go implements evaluation jitter, and ticker/ provides the scheduling tick mechanism.\\n\\n3. **State Manager** (pkg/services/ngalert/state/): manager.go is the central state machine that processes evaluation results and manages alert state transitions. cache.go stores in-memory state, state.go defines the State type, persist.go coordinates state persistence, and three persister implementations (persister_async.go, persister_noop.go, persister_sync.go, persister_sync_rule.go) handle different durability modes.\\n\\n4. **History Writer / Historian** (pkg/services/ngalert/state/historian/): Records state transitions to various backends. backend.go defines the Historian interface, annotation.go writes to Grafana annotations, loki.go writes to a remote Loki instance, prometheus.go writes to Prometheus, multiple.go fans out to multiple backends, noop.go is a no-op backend, and model/ contains the rule model for history entries.\\n\\n5. **Notifier** (pkg/services/ngalert/notifier/): multiorg_alertmanager.go manages per-org Alertmanager instances, alertmanager.go wraps the embedded Alertmanager, redis_peer.go/redis_channel.go implement Redis-based HA clustering, silence_svc.go and receiver_svc.go provide silence/receiver management services. legacy_storage/ handles config persistence.\\n\\n6. **Remote Alertmanager** (pkg/services/ngalert/remote/): Supports forwarding to a remote Mimir-based Alertmanager. remote_primary_forked_alertmanager.go and remote_secondary_forked_alertmanager.go implement forked operation modes. client/ contains the Mimir API client.\\n\\n7. **Sender** (pkg/services/ngalert/sender/): router.go routes alerts to internal or external Alertmanagers, sender.go implements external Alertmanager sending, notifier.go integrates with the Prometheus notifier.\\n\\n8. **Evaluator** (pkg/services/ngalert/eval/): eval.go implements ConditionEval for alert rule condition evaluation, validate.go validates conditions, context.go holds evaluation context.\\n\\n9. **Models** (pkg/services/ngalert/models/): Shared data model types including alert_rule.go, instance.go, alertmanager.go, provisioning.go, silence.go, receivers.go, notifications.go, etc.\\n\\n10. **API** (pkg/services/ngalert/api/): REST API handlers for alerting. api_alertmanager.go, api_ruler.go, api_provisioning.go, api_configuration.go, api_testing.go, api_convert_prometheus.go implement the various API endpoints. forking_alertmanager.go/forking_ruler.go/forking_prometheus.go handle routing between internal and remote backends. tooling/definitions/ contains the OpenAPI type definitions.\\n\\n11. **Provisioning** (pkg/services/ngalert/provisioning/): alert_rules.go, contactpoints.go, templates.go, mute_timings.go, notification_policies.go implement the provisioning API services.\\n\\n12. **Supporting Packages**: image/ (screenshot capture), metrics/ (Prometheus metrics), accesscontrol/ (RBAC), backtesting/ (rule backtesting engine), prom/ (Prometheus rule conversion), lokiconfig/ (Loki configuration), tests/ and testutil/ (test utilities).\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":159,"cache_read_input_tokens":28256,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":159,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"d87c9990-6661-418b-8583-b4975f796820","uuid":"98c4bff9-7553-44ac-8c29-ed8b32161b29"}

contains the history rule model; core.go and dashboard.go are shared utilities; query.go handles history queries.\\n\\n**Notifier** (notifier/): multiorg_alertmanager.go manages per-org Alertmanager receiver_svc.go manage silences and receivers. legacy_storage/ handles legacy config persistence. crypto.go, file_store.go, images.go, templates.go, sender.go, validation.go are supporting components.\\n\\n**Remote Alertmanager** (remote/): Supports remote Mimir-based Alertmanager. remote_primary_forked_alertmanager.go and remote_secondary_forked_alertmanager.go implement forked modes. to internal or external Alertmanagers. sender.go implements ExternalAlertmanager for sending to external AMs. notifier.go and notifier_ext.go integrate with the Prometheus notifier library. \"text\": \"The Grafana unified alerting (ngalert) subsystem is implemented under pkg/services/ngalert/ in sg-evals/grafana--26d36ec. The main entry point is ngalert.go which defines AlertNG, the root service that wires all subsystems.\\n\\n**Alert Rule Storage** (store/): Persists alert rules (alert_rule.go), alert instances (instance_database.go, proto_instance_database.go with protobuf schema in store/proto/v1/alert_rule_state.pb.go), Alertmanager configuration (alertmanager.go), admin configuration (admin_configuration.go), images (image.go), namespace/org info (namespace.go, org.go), and provisioning state (provisioning_store.go). Helper types: models.go, compat.go, deltas.go, transactions.go, range_to_instant.go.\\n\\n**Scheduler** (schedule/): Drives periodic evaluation. schedule.go is the main loop; alert_rule.go is the per-alert-rule goroutine; recording_rule.go handles recording rules; registry.go tracks active rule goroutines; fetcher.go loads rules from storage; jitter.go, retry.go, sequence.go, and ticker/ provide timing utilities; loaded_metrics_reader.go provides metrics.\\n\\n**State Manager** (state/): manager.go processes evaluation results and drives state transitions. cache.go holds in-memory state. state.go defines the State type. persist.go, persister_async.go, persister_noop.go, persister_sync.go, and persister_sync_rule.go implement state persistence strategies. multi_instance_reader.go, compat.go, and template/ support state evaluation.\\n\\n**History Writer / Historian** (state/historian/): Records state-change history. backend.go defines the Historian interface. annotation.go writes to Grafana annotations, loki.go writes to remote Loki, prometheus.go writes to Prometheus, multiple.go fans out to multiple backends, noop.go is a no-op. model/ contains the history rule model; core.go and dashboard.go are shared utilities; query.go handles history queries.\\n\\n**Notifier** (notifier/): multiorg_alertmanager.go manages per-org Alertmanager instances. alertmanager.go wraps the embedded Alertmanager. autogen_alertmanager.go auto-generates default configs. redis_peer.go/redis_channel.go provide Redis HA clustering. silence_svc.go and receiver_svc.go manage silences and receivers. legacy_storage/ handles legacy config persistence. crypto.go, file_store.go, images.go, templates.go, sender.go, validation.go are supporting components.\\n\\n**Remote Alertmanager** (remote/): Supports remote Mimir-based Alertmanager. remote_primary_forked_alertmanager.go and remote_secondary_forked_alertmanager.go implement forked modes. client/ contains the Mimir API client (alertmanager.go, alertmanager_configuration.go, alertmanager_state.go, mimir.go, mimir_auth_round_tripper.go).\\n\\n**Sender** (sender/): router.go routes alerts to internal or external Alertmanagers. sender.go implements ExternalAlertmanager for sending to external AMs. notifier.go and notifier_ext.go integrate with the Prometheus notifier library. slog_adapter.go bridges logging.\\n\\n**Evaluator** (eval/): eval.go implements ConditionEval for alert rule conditions. validate.go validates conditions. context.go holds evaluation context. extract_md.go extracts metadata.\\n\\n**Models** (models/): Shared data types: alert_rule.go, alert_query.go, instance.go, instance_labels.go, alertmanager.go, provisioning.go, silence.go, receivers.go, notifications.go, history.go, image.go, admin_configuration.go, permissions.go, accesscontrol.go, constants.go, errors.go, fingerprint.go, time.go.\\n\\n**API** (api/): REST API layer. api_alertmanager.go, api_ruler.go, api_provisioning.go, api_configuration.go, api_testing.go, api_convert_prometheus.go, api_ruler_history.go, api_ruler_export.go, api_alertmanager_silences.go implement endpoints. forking_alertmanager.go, forking_ruler.go, forking_prometheus.go handle routing. lotex_am.go, lotex_ruler.go, lotex_prom.go proxy to remote data sources. generated_base_api_*.go are auto-generated stubs. tooling/definitions/ contains OpenAPI type definitions. compat/, hcl/, prometheus/, validation/ are sub-packages.\\n\\n**Provisioning** (provisioning/): alert_rules.go, contactpoints.go, templates.go, mute_timings.go, notification_policies.go implement the provisioning API services. validation/ checks provenance. compat.go bridges formats.\\n\\n**Supporting packages**: image/ (screenshot capture service), metrics/ (Prometheus metrics for all subsystems), accesscontrol/ (RBAC for rules, receivers, silences), backtesting/ (rule backtesting engine), prom/
